        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16359109-k?shelf=arrogant-hero">arrogant-hero</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer515147000" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16483128162656495991"><b>4.5 You're My Home Stars!</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1386058758i/7282662.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>"I could spend the rest of my life inside you and die happy. You’re my home."</b><br/><br/><i>Gabriel's Redemption</i> is the beautiful conclusion to the epic love story of Julia and Gabriel Emerson. The story continues with its redemption based theme in this final installment. While this was by far my least favorite book in the series I still really enjoyed it and I am heartbroken to see it end! I felt that there were some things that could have been executed better which prevented me from </span>
  <span id="freeText16483128162656495991" style="display:none"><b>4.5 You're My Home Stars!</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1386058758i/7282662.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>"I could spend the rest of my life inside you and die happy. You’re my home."</b><br><br><i>Gabriel's Redemption</i> is the beautiful conclusion to the epic love story of Julia and Gabriel Emerson. The story continues with its redemption based theme in this final installment. While this was by far my least favorite book in the series I still really enjoyed it and I am heartbroken to see it end! I felt that there were some things that could have been executed better which prevented me from giving this book 5 stars. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ I don't like the lack of epilogue! Does Julia become a Professor? Do Paul and Julia remain friends? What happens with Simon? Does he get the girl back or suffer alone? Do Aaron and Rachel ever have kids? What happens with Julia's little brother, does the surgery work? Also one of the things that bugged me the most was the lack of oral sex on Julia's part. I felt that since she had been degraded in the past I thought we were going to have a scene of her overcoming her fears and giving Gabriel a blow job. I didn't want the scene just for the sex, I wanted it to be shown as a sign of growth on Julia's part. Also, there was the scene where Gabriel thought Julia was dead. Now this was a huge problem to me. That scene could have been better executed and had more emotion. It didn't, and I just felt that it was out of character for Gabriel to handle is so well. That's NOT the fierce Professor that I know and love! Oh well... <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> This series has always held a special place in my heart and it probably will for a long time to come. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"For you, my love, I would endeavor to pluck the stars from the sky, only to shower them at your feet."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1386659119i/7416868.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Redemption picks up with Gabriel and Julia married, together and blissfully happy. Julia is hard at work to attain her degree, and Gabriel is teaching. There's still some hardships and secrets, but for the most part married life is going really well for them! <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"I won’t find happiness without you.”<br>“For how can a man live without his heart?"</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1386660143i/7416947.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The love that is shared between Julia and Gabriel is really awe-inspiring to read about. I'm not married and I'll admit after reading a love like Gabriel and Julia's I don't know how anyone will ever add up to The Professor's love for Julia. Their love is so sweet, fierce, protective, passionate, tender, sexy and consuming all at the same time! I just soaked it all up! <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"If you were Francis to my Guido da Montefeltro, you’d come for my soul, wouldn’t you?"</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1386661535i/7417207.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Before anyone thinks that Gabriel and Julia's love is too perfect, let me stop you right there! One of the things that I loved so much about this book was how realistic everything was. Their relationship isn't perfect. While they love each other fiercely, both of them still make mistakes and they do fight at times, but they always make up and learn from the mistakes they make. Before they can get their HEA after though obstacles and questions arise from Gabriel's past that he has to be able to overcome if he wants to move forward with his life with Julia. Will they get their HEA? Or is there love destined to be tragic like Beatrice and Dante's...?<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“You think of everything.”<br>“I simply think of you. You are everything.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1386663695i/7417524.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>In conclusion, Gabriel's Redemption was a very good conclusion to a series that I would recommend to everyone! The writing style of Sylvain Reynard is so poetic and beautiful that I can't imagine anyone finding fault in it. And last but not least lets not forget about Professor Gabriel Emerson. Let's all be honest ladies, he made this series! Without him our hearts wouldn't have swooned and I wouldn't have gone on a David Gandy hunt looking for all my perfect Gabriel pictures! Gabriel's character was so perfectly written and executed. His love and devotion to Julia make him one of the best book boyfriends of all time and I teared up just reading abut the love he had for her. If you haven't read this series yet, GO PICK THEM UP RIGHT NOW! <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>Of all the gifts God gave me, he thought, the greatest one is you.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><b>
  <i>
    <br>

<div id="review_597117575" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/597117575" />
    <a title="Allison ❤️Will Never Conquer Her TBR❤️" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9080319-allison-will-never-conquer-her-tbr"><img alt="Allison ❤️Will Never Conquer Her TBR❤️" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1465384674p2/9080319.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/597117575?book_show_action=true">Apr 22, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Allison ❤️Will Never Conquer Her TBR❤️" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Allison ❤️Will Never Conquer Her TBR❤️" href="/user/show/9080319-allison-will-never-conquer-her-tbr">Allison ❤️Will Never Conquer Her TBR❤️</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer597117575" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9577311271041687402"><a href='http://s1320.photobucket.com/albums/u538/allipalk/Used%20in%20review/?action=view&current=2285455a42344b9ada3c90d54951142f_zps6b8e91cf.jpg' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1386439269i/7364913._SX540_.jpg' alt='Photobucket Pictures, Images and Photos' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>I've one thing to say- Sylvain Reynard didn't plan to write this book. He wrote Gabriel's Rapture in the hopes that The Professor and Julia's story would be complete. It's the readers that pushed for this book. They wanted more from this couple...a look into their future a few years down the road. To give us a sense of closure. SR gave us this in spades! Not only did we get the COMPLETE HEA for Gabriel and Julianne, but closure to each and every nuance to their story. Of Rachel and Aaron, he</span>
  <span id="freeText9577311271041687402" style="display:none"><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/albums/u538/allipalk/Used%20in%20review/?action=view&amp;current=2285455a42344b9ada3c90d54951142f_zps6b8e91cf.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1386439269i/7364913._SX540_.jpg" alt="Photobucket Pictures, Images and Photos" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I've one thing to say- Sylvain Reynard didn't plan to write this book. He wrote Gabriel's Rapture in the hopes that The Professor and Julia's story would be complete. It's the readers that pushed for this book. They wanted more from this couple...a look into their future a few years down the road. To give us a sense of closure. SR gave us this in spades! Not only did we get the COMPLETE HEA for Gabriel and Julianne, but closure to each and every nuance to their story. Of Rachel and Aaron, her father Tom and his new happenings, of Paul, of Natalie and Simon. Every detail of closure handed over to his readers in all his poetic perfection. <br><br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/albums/u538/allipalk/Used%20in%20review/?action=view&amp;current=de25433776389a69bdf63be5f84331b3_zps9a06f85b.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1386439716i/7365250._SX540_.jpg" alt="Photobucket Pictures, Images and Photos" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Were parts of the book a bit long or anticlimactic for me? Yes. Were there parts I felt a bit too religious or spiritual for those who don't believe? Maybe. I can't complain there as I think it added a true sense of person, of beliefs and hopes that there's powers beyond our control...something to pray for and thank blessings for. Aside from that, the only other thing I found myself wishing for was more steamy love scenes. It always bothered me this series was tagged erotica because I don't see it at all....or that it was recommended for lovers of all things FSoG. I find this book totally different. Much more beautifully romantic and less smutty. That being said, a little more steam would've been the icing on my Gabriel cake! I mean, they had orchard sex, museum sex, kitchen counter sex, chocolate body painting sex....*wipes brow*..and desk sex!!!! More deets SR!<br><br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/albums/u538/allipalk/Gifs%20from%20AE/?action=view&amp;current=makingoutkitchencounter_zpsabdd190a.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380419350ra/831243.gif" alt="Photobucket Pictures, Images and Photos" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Sylvain Reynard is truly one of my favorite authors. This series being my favorite love story of all time. To take such torturous pasts and circumstances and give us their story come full circle, my opinion stays strong...Gabriel and Julianne are my favorite. The author truly knows his Dante and there were parts I found myself skimming when she was doing her speech, or some of the poetry. It's a bit over this blonde's head I guess. But the beauty of his writing remains. Rumor has it, he's venturing into more PNR writing. A shame but I wish all the success in the future to a writer that has touched me like few can.<br><br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/albums/u538/allipalk/Used%20in%20review/?action=view&amp;current=0558890424039dc9ffba44f8be830115_zps6246a320.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1386440885i/7365891._SY540_.jpg" alt="Photobucket Pictures, Images and Photos" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/albums/u538/allipalk/Used%20in%20review/?action=view&amp;current=0f0897ac7f6b3752f8ac72ada10d2c5c_zps102875ac.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379798144i/636428._SX540_.jpg" alt="Photobucket Pictures, Images and Photos" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="http://s1320.photobucket.com/albums/u538/allipalk/Used%20in%20review/?action=view&amp;current=7c3d60906f86cb450646b0d67c607527_zps9acadc77.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1386439435i/7364942._SY540_.jpg" alt="Photobucket Pictures, Images and Photos" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer609117545" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer13321377757155000724"><b>ARC provided by author in exchange for honest review</b><br/><br/><b>4.5~5 Man of Steel stars </b><br/><br/>What can I say but I LOVED this series and I fell in love Gabriel Emerson all over again. To say I’m sad to see this series conclude is an understatement, I just didn't want to say goodbye to Professor Gabriel Emerson and Julianne just yet. Gabriel’s Redemption was a beautiful conclusion to a heartfelt journey of two individuals who had overcome their past, demons, and addictions and found redemption in forgiveness, lov</span>
  <span id="freeText13321377757155000724" style="display:none"><b>ARC provided by author in exchange for honest review</b><br><br><b>4.5~5 Man of Steel stars </b><br><br>What can I say but I LOVED this series and I fell in love Gabriel Emerson all over again. To say I’m sad to see this series conclude is an understatement, I just didn't want to say goodbye to Professor Gabriel Emerson and Julianne just yet. Gabriel’s Redemption was a beautiful conclusion to a heartfelt journey of two individuals who had overcome their past, demons, and addictions and found redemption in forgiveness, love, faith and hope in each other. The road to redemption is never easy, but it is attainable.<br><br><a href="http://www.flickr.com/photos/66034700@N08/11128003686/" title="GabrielsRedemption-3 by ms.meesh, on Flickr" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1385790923i/7228755.jpg" width="363" height="500" alt="GabrielsRedemption-3" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>
  <i>“I’ve loved him since I was seventeen. I love all of him – the light and the dark, the good and the bad. That’s why he’s with me. He left the others behind and he will never go back.” ~Julianne<br><br>“Charity is a great virtue, and so is faith. But hope means the most to me. This is hope.”</i>
</b><br><br><a href="http://www.flickr.com/photos/66034700@N08/11128004356/" title="Gabriel's-4 by ms.meesh, on Flickr" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1385790923i/7228756.jpg" width="336" height="500" alt="Gabriel's-4" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Gabriel’s Redemption picks up six months later after the Emerson’s wedding. Julianne is finishing up her first year of her PhD program at Harvard and Gabriel is now a professor at Boston University. They are living the newlywed life, romance and lots of unbelievably hot great sex. (I mean lots of passionate sex!) Not is all peaches and cream for the Emersons, Julianne is trying to balancing her academic career and her duties as a wife. As for Gabriel, his past demons and addiction still haunts him. <br><br>As they settled into their married life, Gabriel feels its time to expand their family and are ready for kids. Julianne, on the other hand, wants kids but not at the moment. She wants to finish her PhD program before they expand their family. Gabriel does not pressure Julianne but she is left feeling torn.<br><br><a href="http://www.flickr.com/photos/66034700@N08/11128003376/" title="gabriel-6 by ms.meesh, on Flickr" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1385790923i/7228757.jpg" width="340" height="500" alt="gabriel-6" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>After a series of events, Gabriel’s starts to wonder if he is even worthy of that second chance to be a father again. His past and demons that he tried to put behind him slowly creeps and plagues his mind and torments his soul. He has a lot of demons to fight so he finally decides that he needs to put them to a rest so he can give his all to his new life and marriage. With this, Gabriel starts to make amends with the people that he has hurt and with himself and begins his search on his biological parents’ history. As much as Julianne wants to help Gabriel, he feels that there are times he must do it alone. <br><br><a href="http://www.flickr.com/photos/66034700@N08/11128003606/" title="Gabriel-5 by ms.meesh, on Flickr" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1385790923i/7228758.jpg" width="500" height="334" alt="Gabriel-5" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>As for Julianne, she is no longer the shy innocent girl we saw in Gabriel’s Inferno. She has blossomed into a beautiful independent woman. She has made a name for herself in the academia world. In this book, we see a stronger Julianne, who will fight for her dreams, family and her love for Gabriel. Her heart can be only described as pure. She didn’t care what anyone thought of her husband because in her heart and mind, Gabriel is indeed worthy of love and redemption. The connection that they hold is so deep, intense and strong that nothing can tear them apart even with old enemies still lurking around. <br><br><a href="http://www.flickr.com/photos/66034700@N08/11128150483/" title="GabrielsRedemption-2 by ms.meesh, on Flickr" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1385790923i/7228759.jpg" width="490" height="500" alt="GabrielsRedemption-2" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>There is no question that these two are perfectly suited for each other. She is the ying to his yang. They are two peas in a pod. She is his Beatrice and he is her Dante. The love that have for each other radiates from the pages. It is as if the stars have aligned, and they are fated one another and nothing can tear them apart. I absolutely love that no matter what arguments, misunderstanding, and whatever problems that stands in their way, they stand side by side and show a united front. They support each other, defend each other and love each other unconditionally. <br><br><a href="http://www.flickr.com/photos/66034700@N08/11128045004/" title="GabrielRedemption-1 by ms.meesh, on Flickr" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1385790923i/7228760.jpg" width="345" height="500" alt="GabrielRedemption-1" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>
  <i>"For you, my love, I would endeavor to pluck the stars from the sky, only to shower them at your feet."</i>
</b><br><br>Gabriel’s Redemption was simply beautifully well written and left me crying happy tears. This book is about making amends with the past, accepting what can’t be changed, moving forward, and of course, LOVE. Love can heal old wounds and scars. It doesn't always come easy. Love is overcoming obstacles, facing challenges, fighting to be together, holding on &amp; never letting go. It is a short word, easy to spell, difficult to define, and impossible to live without. In Gabriel’s Redemption, the <b> LOVE</b> between Gabriel and Julianne was the kind of love that can move mountains. Gabriel clearly worships the ground Julianne walks on. She is his life and vice versa. After what Gabriel and Julianne had experienced, their love story had come to a full circle. At the end of the last page, I was at peace knowing that their love triumphed and overcame all the odds that were thrown at them. Their love was so passionate, tender, fierce, unconditional, and all-consuming. They never, ever stopped fighting for each other and they were truly destined and made for each other. The love between Gabriel and Julianne is the kind of true love that everyone wants and hopefully can experience in their life. <br><br><b>
  <i>"You think of everything." "I simply think of you. you are my everything."<br><br>“Now my Blessedness appears.”</i>
</b>~Gabriel Emerson<br><br>Thank you, Mr. Reynard for introducing us to the Professor and Julianne and allowing us to accompany them on their beautiful journey of forgiveness, strength, hope, courage, perseverance, redemption, and love. All I can ask of Mr. Reynard is for a novella...I need more Gabriel and Julianne. I just don’t want to say goodbye to them just yet. It was an emotional sweet journey that it’s bittersweet to see Gabriel’s and and Julianne story come to an end. <br><br>So I highly recommend everyone to read this book and series. You will not be disappointed with the Professor. <br><br><a href="http://www.flickr.com/photos/66034700@N08/11127974825/" title="gabrielscollage by ms.meesh, on Flickr" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1385790923i/7228761.jpg" width="500" height="375" alt="gabrielscollage" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/4562483.Sylvain_Reynard" title="Sylvain Reynard" rel="nofollow noopener">Sylvain Reynard</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="13321377757155000724" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_772971738" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/772971738" />
    <a title="Jessica" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2821605-jessica"><img alt="Jessica" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1380497282p2/2821605.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/772971738?book_show_action=true">Nov 24, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jessica" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jessica" href="/user/show/2821605-jessica">Jessica</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2821605-jessica?shelf=blog-review">blog-review</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer772971738" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16309048093238312925">Sylvain Reynard’s GABRIEL'S REDEMPTION is the highly anticipated final book in the Gabriel’s Inferno series. The series was originally conceived as two books, but Reynard changed his mind after readers pleaded for a third. If you haven’t read the series, I do recommend you read the first two books before proceeding to REDEMPTION because Reynard does revisit past characters and gives you character backgrounds that will leave you lost otherwise.<br/><br/>Before I proceed to the review, I want to say, that i</span>
  <span id="freeText16309048093238312925" style="display:none">Sylvain Reynard’s GABRIEL'S REDEMPTION is the highly anticipated final book in the Gabriel’s Inferno series. The series was originally conceived as two books, but Reynard changed his mind after readers pleaded for a third. If you haven’t read the series, I do recommend you read the first two books before proceeding to REDEMPTION because Reynard does revisit past characters and gives you character backgrounds that will leave you lost otherwise.<br /><br />Before I proceed to the review, I want to say, that it pains me to give this book the rating I do, because I adored GABRIEL'S INFERNO and really enjoyed GABRIEL'S RAPTURE. Alas, I’m in the minority that didn’t enjoy GABRIEL'S REDEMPTION.<br /><br />What I did like was the softening of Gabriel in a particular scene involving an orphanage and being called Superman by the children. I really liked seeing Gabriel out of his element and finally putting the past regarding Maia away. I just adored seeing Julia presenting at Oxford. I cheered for her as she delivered her first paper and high-fived her when she was able to handle her own regarding Christa and her questions. I do believe we needed this scene in order for Gabriel to realize how amazing Julia is in the academic world when given a little space.<br /><br />Ultimately, what didn’t work for me was how clichéd GABRIEL'S REDEMPTION was. Julia doesn’t want a baby and wants to focus on school, but Gabriel wants one. I’ll leave out what happens so you’re not spoiled, but I’m so disappointed because I understand Julia’s worry. It’s one I’ve had for her since she married Gabriel because I know women in academia having children and how it postpones a lot for them. Several good friends got pregnant during their final coursework for the PhD and several years later still aren’t done. So my worry for Julia is perfectly justified and I know she’ll have a good career regardless of the outcome, but I wanted so much more for her. I wanted Gabriel to want more for her too and in the end, I was disappointed. The first two books in the series left me emotionally drained and I cared about the fate of each character, but midway through GABRIEL'S REDEMPTION, I couldn’t summon the energy to care. Also, Reynard attempts to give closure to every character. So if you’ve been wondering what happens to Simon or Natalie, you’ll get closure, but the way Reynard works them into the narrative, it’s not related to Julia and Gabriel’s story. While it’s nice that he goes back to tie up lose ends, I feel at times that like real life some answers aren’t known and that’s the beauty of life. Furthermore, there are still some unanswered questions regarding a few characters. I have a feeling Reynard will be revisiting Paul in his next novel.<br /><br />In the end, I just feel GABRIEL'S REDEMPTION was lackluster. It read like a long epilogue that just wouldn’t end. Julia and Gabriel fight, she locks herself in the bathroom, make up sex ensues, and repeat this scene a few more times. I know newlyweds have sex, but Reynard has these two fornicating left and right that I’m surprised Julia can even walk the next day much less get out bed. At one point, Gabriel is impatient because Julia announces she’s menstruating and while he understands, he’s busy counting down the days to sexy time. I’m surprised he doesn’t have her menstruation cycle memorized. I know readers asked for a third novel, but in this case, I do feel that an epilogue or a novella would have been more than fine.<br /><br />Die hard Gabrielites will no doubt love GABRIEL'S REDEMPTION. If you’re unsure about picking this up, I recommend reading a sample first and maybe a few reviews in order to determine your interest or borrow a copy from a friend.<br /><br />This review and more are posted at <a href="http://literaryetc.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Literary, etc</a>.</span>
  <a data-text-id="16309048093238312925" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <span id="freeText16022025757629363536" style="display:none"><b>5 Redeeming Stars!!</b>	<br><br>I’ll be very short on this one because there’s nothing more I can say except that I really loved this book. <br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1388016904i/7721827.jpg" width="300" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>In this book we have a happily married Gabriel and Julia but their happy ever after is far from coming, since they still have a lot of unresolved issues. <br>Starting with their past and through all the doubts about their future, the lovers still have a bumpy road ahead of them. <br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1387327417i/7578640.jpg" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This was probably the best one for me. <br>The writing style was flawless, as always and all the issues I had in the second installment disappeared in this one.       <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="✝✝ Ⓓaisy ❣ ✝✝ " class="user" itemprop="url" name="✝✝ Ⓓaisy ❣ ✝✝ " href="/user/show/5629016-aisy">✝✝ Ⓓaisy ❣ ✝✝ </a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer560788857" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10115484932647755954"><br/><a href='http://s799.photobucket.com/user/79twilightlover/media/Bully/oRLsHXe.gif.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1386256900ra/7323112.gif' alt=' photo oRLsHXe.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><b> <i> THIS BOOK WAS SIMPLY WOW, AMAZING AND BRILLIANT!!! </i></b> <br/><br/>Sylvain Reynard,<br/><br/><a href='http://s799.photobucket.com/user/79twilightlover/media/Bully/giphy.gif.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1386256904ra/7323115.gif' alt=' photo giphy.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>My emotions were literally snowballed from happiness to sadness. One series that never failed!!! <br/><br/>When Christa came in and couldn't shut that nasty mouth of hers, I was <br/><br/><a href='http://s799.photobucket.com/user/79twilightlover/media/Bully/wnI0ang.gif.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1339919088?book_show_action=true">Jul 19, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " href="/user/show/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie">Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/18368537-gabriel-s-redemption">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie?shelf=read-in-2015">read-in-2015</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1339919088" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15388092949735704291">Gabriel and Julia are both in Boston and doing well in their pursuits. Their marriage is going well but as always, Gabriel wants <i>more</i> and we all know that he usually gets his way!<br/><br/>Well, I'm happy to say that nothing too crazy happens in this book. Now that doesn't mean there isn't drama because of course there is. <br/><br/>Some issue comes up that causes Gabriel to want to search his past and find out things. And unfortunately it causes him to revert to some bad past behaviors. I was happy that he only di</span>
  <span id="freeText15388092949735704291" style="display:none">Gabriel and Julia are both in Boston and doing well in their pursuits. Their marriage is going well but as always, Gabriel wants <i>more</i> and we all know that he usually gets his way!<br><br>Well, I'm happy to say that nothing too crazy happens in this book. Now that doesn't mean there isn't drama because of course there is. <br><br>Some issue comes up that causes Gabriel to want to search his past and find out things. And unfortunately it causes him to revert to some bad past behaviors. I was happy that he only did what he did! <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1437767704i/15626974.jpg" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Julia is a wonderful wife...just like we knew she would be, definitely a bit old fashioned. I was a little surprised at her complete forgetfulness but you just knew that was coming. <br><br>And for the most part, this book read like a really long epilogue. We find out what happens with Paul, Christa and Simon and the rest of Gabriel and Julia's families. <br><br>The ending was sweet...my heart went out to poor Gabriel but I'm glad things worked out. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1437459306i/15587121._SY540_.jpg" width="200" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <u>Favorite quote:</u>
</b><br><br>♥ "If you don't know how this happened, darling, then clearly I'm not doing it right."</span>

              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2371593588820258321"><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>“Sometimes, you should let the nastiness speak for itself.”</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br/><br/>A gazzilliion stars for this book!<br/><br/><a href='http://photobucket.com/images/Happy%20Dance%20gif' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/453601.gif' alt='Happy Dance gif photo: tumblr_ledfmelsvK1qd3url.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>I really, really want to cry because it just ended. It's just so <b>BEAUTIFUL</b>.<br/><br/><a href='http://s725.photobucket.com/user/Kristin90183/media/GR%20Stuff/Book%20Boyfriends%20with%20D/Beautiful.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380431020i/864651.jpg' alt=' photo Beautiful.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>If I could just stretch the story forever, I would be so happy.<br/><br/><i>
  <blockquote>“Every night when I fall asleep with her in my arms, I thank God she’s mine. Every morning when I wake up, my first thought is that I’m grateful she married me. I will never be worthy of her. But I spend every day trying my damnedest."</blockquote>
</i><br/><br/>The story </span>
  <span id="freeText2371593588820258321" style="display:none"><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>“Sometimes, you should let the nastiness speak for itself.”</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br><br>A gazzilliion stars for this book!<br><br><a href="http://photobucket.com/images/Happy%20Dance%20gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/453601.gif" alt="Happy Dance gif photo: tumblr_ledfmelsvK1qd3url.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I really, really want to cry because it just ended. It's just so <b>BEAUTIFUL</b>.<br><br><a href="http://s725.photobucket.com/user/Kristin90183/media/GR%20Stuff/Book%20Boyfriends%20with%20D/Beautiful.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380431020i/864651.jpg" alt=" photo Beautiful.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>If I could just stretch the story forever, I would be so happy.<br><br><i>
  <blockquote>“Every night when I fall asleep with her in my arms, I thank God she’s mine. Every morning when I wake up, my first thought is that I’m grateful she married me. I will never be worthy of her. But I spend every day trying my damnedest."</blockquote>
</i><br><br>The story continues after the marriage of Gabriel and Julienne. In this story, Gabriel wants to have kids. But Julianne feels as if she's not yet ready to have a family, she thinks she's selfish for her actions. Old enemies resurface and insecurities arises. The pressure is on.<br><br><i>
  <blockquote>“Of all the gifts God gave me, he thought, the greatest one is you.”</blockquote>
</i><br><br>Beautiful, alluring and oh-so-freaking genius. I think SR did a great job of writing this book. I love how the writer actually quotes about history, anecdotes, poems, quotable quotes and some I-have-never-heard-of this-before-now-I-know stories. Man, I love how <i>Il Professore</i> just spout out his love for Julianne. For example:<br><br><blockquote>“For you, my love, I would endeavor to pluck the stars from the sky, only to shower them at your feet.”</blockquote><br><br>See what I mean? I think he just melted the North AND South pole.<br><br>Oh Gabriel...<br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380435911ra/880863.gif" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><a href="http://photobucket.com/images/feels%20gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380432758ra/870393.gif" alt="feels gif photo: HOW DO I HOLD IN THESE FEELS HOWDOIHOLDINTHESEFEELS.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>And also melted the coldest of cold hearts. <br><br>I love you.<br><br>PLUS! Julianne's fiyaaaaaaaah!<br><br><blockquote>“You’re right about one thing, though.”<br>“And what’s that?” Christa sounded contemptuous.<br>Julia smiled knowingly. “My husband is an exceptional lover. He’s attentive, creative, and absolutely mind-blowing. And tonight and every night, the woman enjoying his adventurous nature will be me.”<br>She gave Christa a long look.<br>“Not bad for a mouse.”</blockquote><br><br><a href="http://photobucket.com/images/feels%20gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1387632837ra/7637628.gif" alt="feels gif photo: Funny gif feels-1.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="http://photobucket.com/images/bitch%20gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1387633539ra/7638256.gif" alt="bitch gif photo: bitch.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="http://photobucket.com/images/bitch%20gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <span>[image error]</span>
</a><br><br><a href="http://photobucket.com/images/bitch%20gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380231773ra/681305.gif" alt="bitch gif photo: Stupid bitch gif 115.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="http://photobucket.com/images/bitch%20gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1387633539ra/7638257.gif" alt="bitch gif photo: bitchslappin smosh-gif-bitch.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>TAKE THAT CHRISTA!<br><br><b>HOORAY FOR JULIANNE!</b><br><br><a href="http://photobucket.com/images/minions%20gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/507728.gif" alt="minions gif photo: despicable me minions audience gif tumblr_leiwr7Jj9e1qe94gj.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>All in all, I would say this is one awesome, heartbreaking book. The book grips you until the very end. I think I had a solid five hours sleep just wanting to finish this. My Mom got mad 'cause I wasn't sleeping yet and I had to wake up early the next morning. But you know what?<br><br><a href="http://photobucket.com/images/i%20regret%20nothing%20gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380387972ra/748272.gif" alt="i regret nothing gif photo: Doctor Who I Regret Nothing gif MWLUe.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>There were some characters I wanted them to have a nice ending but really focused on Gabriel and Julianne more. I think it would be nice if Simon had his own happy ending <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/4562483.Sylvain_Reynard" title="Sylvain Reynard" rel="nofollow noopener">Sylvain Reynard</a>…? Just a thought but it's up to you. :)<br><br>Thank you for this wonderful trilogy! Hope to read the next book of yours.<br><br><br><br><br>My face when I heard it would be published on December 2013:<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380408344ra/798757.gif" width="600" height="600" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br><br><br><br>Feb 6, 2013<br>Oh sh*t. Oh sh*t!<br>There's a book 3!!!!!!!<br>Oh I <b>love</b> this series. :)</span>
  <a data-text-id="2371593588820258321" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_483330651" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/483330651" />

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog?shelf=anxiously-awaiting-release-date">anxiously-awaiting-release-date</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog?shelf=top-fantasy-boyfriends">top-fantasy-boyfriends</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer483330651" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16440938979930043394">4 Stars!!!<br/>(BR with Melissa)<br/><br/>Well, it seemed that we waited a long time for the release of "Gabriel's Redemption".<br/>I really enjoyed this final installment.<br/>Was it as good as the first two books, in my opinion? No.<br/>It was good but I just feel like something was missing.<br/><br/>Maybe a little too much Dante talk?<br/>I loved Gabriel.<br/>Without a doubt, he's still my #2 book boyfriend.<br/>The man has a sexual appetite that won't quit and is the master at the art of seduction.<br/>I wished the sexy time scenes had more heat to t</span>
  <span id="freeText16440938979930043394" style="display:none">4 Stars!!!<br>(BR with Melissa)<br><br>Well, it seemed that we waited a long time for the release of "Gabriel's Redemption".<br>I really enjoyed this final installment.<br>Was it as good as the first two books, in my opinion? No.<br>It was good but I just feel like something was missing.<br><br>Maybe a little too much Dante talk?<br>I loved Gabriel.<br>Without a doubt, he's still my #2 book boyfriend.<br>The man has a sexual appetite that won't quit and is the master at the art of seduction.<br>I wished the sexy time scenes had more heat to them.<br><br><br><a href="http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/image_zps6386dceb.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1386212426i/7313353._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo image_zps6386dceb.jpg" width="350 height=" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>Julia, she's still very much annoying.<br>The woman needs to stand up for herself!!<br>I loved that Katherine Picton was back in this one and she basically told Julia she needs to start defending herself.<br>I believe she meant against people like Christa Peterson, but no, the person she stands up to is Gabriel.<br>I felt he was trying hard to battle his inner demons and he wanted so desperately to start a family with Julia, but she spent most of the time having anxiety over having children and finishing her studies at Harvard.<br><br><br><br><a href="http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/image_zps054cadaa.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1386212426i/7313354._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo image_zps054cadaa.jpg" width="350" height="450" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><br>The story still has the couple very much in love and boy they spend most of their time sexing it up.<br>I think maybe because there wasn't the angst we had in the first two books, that the book seemed to drag.<br>We do get to find out about things that were never revealed in the previous books, like what Gabriel wrote in that card he sent with flowers to Julia, after he found out she was his Beatrice.<br>We learn why Simon and Natalie stayed away from Julia.<br>Most importantly, some of the characters get what they deserve and a few get closure, like Paulina.<br>I loved that this was in the book.<br>Yes, she was a bitch, but Gabriel treated her so horribly.<br>That had to be a part of his redemption.<br><br><br><a href="http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/image_zps28fb86be.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1386212426i/7313355._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo image_zps28fb86be.jpg" width="350" height="450" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><br><br>Even though Grace passed on, she still was very present in this book.<br>She was like their guardian angel.<br>I loved Richard.<br>He always had the best advice and there was a very touching scene with him that people might find corny, but I loved it.<br><br><br><a href="http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/image_zps83d4d2e0.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1386212426i/7313356._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo image_zps83d4d2e0.jpg" width="350" height="500" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>So I gave this a 4 because I love my Gabriel and he made me swoon several times.<br>Plus I love how he actually did change a lot and he saw the error of his ways in the past and he made a conscious effort to change and make amends. <br>Plus he LOVES giving Oral to Julia!!! LOL<br>You will know what I'm talking about when you get towards the end of the story.<br><br>That bit at the end, I feel Gabriel almost had a lackluster response to the situation, which was odd. That part could have been a real tear jerker.<br>I'm sad to have to say goodbye to Gabriel.<br>He was the first to knock Christian Grey off the #1 spot as my book boyfriend.<br>He's the #1 hottest bow tie wearing Professor!!!<br>I realized after reading Gabriel's Inferno &amp; Gabriel's Rapture, that there were indeed great books out there like the FSOG series.<br>So I will always be thankful to Sylvain Reynard for that. :)<br><br><br><i>
  <b>"Don't cry, my sweet girl. You're my Beatrice and my sticky little leaf and my beautiful wife. I'm sorry I've been such a bastard. I wanted to show you how important you are to me. You are my most precious masterpiece."</b>
</i> - Gabriel<br><br><br><br><i>
  <b>"This is the culmination of all my hopes, Gabriel."</b>
</i> <b>Julia reached out to him and he strained to catch her pinky finger with his own.</b> <i>
  <b>"This is my happy ending."</b>
</i> - Julia</span>

<div id="review_529738741" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/529738741" />
    <a title="Michelle" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13126896-michelle"><img alt="Michelle" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1505605297p2/13126896.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/529738741?book_show_action=true">Feb 07, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Michelle" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Michelle" href="/user/show/13126896-michelle">Michelle</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer529738741" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer927517504016758848"><br/>The conclusion of Julia & Gabriel’s story was just as magical as the first two in this series. A romance destined between two lost souls that find their home within each other’s arms.<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1386550730i/7389469.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/>Gabriel & Julia are making a home amidst the struggle of her studies to gain her PhD. Newly married, these two have given one another the strength to heal most of the scars of their past. But when Gabriel shares his desire to start a family with Julia, a few fears not yet forgotten surface. <br/><br/>Wanting a family brings </span>
  <span id="freeText927517504016758848" style="display:none"><br>The conclusion of Julia &amp; Gabriel’s story was just as magical as the first two in this series. A romance destined between two lost souls that find their home within each other’s arms.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1386550730i/7389469.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Gabriel &amp; Julia are making a home amidst the struggle of her studies to gain her PhD. Newly married, these two have given one another the strength to heal most of the scars of their past. But when Gabriel shares his desire to start a family with Julia, a few fears not yet forgotten surface. <br><br>Wanting a family brings new and old fears to light for both Julia &amp; Gabriel. Julia’s focus is her studies. Her desire to finish her program first and fearing disappointing Gabriel if she puts her dreams before his happiness. Gabriel has had no desire to seek out his own bloodline, but the thought of a child of his own forces him to walk down a path that awakens sleeping demons. For both Julia &amp; Gabriel, the fear of losing what you love is at the heart of this story. The fear of putting your faith into something you can’t control and risking having it torn from your grasp. <br><br><i>
  <b> “Of all the gifts God gave me, he thought, the greatest one is you.”</b>
</i> <br><br>Gabriel has become a changed man since Julia. She saved his life all those years ago in an orchard when he thought she was a vision and then years later when he realized his Beatrice was real. But his redemption cannot simply be found in his actions, it must be found through forgiveness. <br><br>But this is not just the story of these two. We get a look into the lives of all the players that have been with us on this journey. Some loved and some not so much. But nothing is left unresolved. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1386550730i/7389470.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>I cannot even begin to explain how much I loved this series. I absolutely adore classic literature and romance, this is the perfect mix of both in how it is written and the theme of Dante &amp; Beatrice. <br><br><i>
  <b> “Have you ever made love in an orchard before? Her eyes widened and she shook her head. “Then I’m glad I’m your first.” She tightened her grip on his hand. “You’re my last, Gabriel. My only.”</b>
</i> <br><br>I was so glad to see that everything was resolved and the way that the author placed in the stories from the other characters, adding in a bit of suspense as to what was to come was utterly brilliant. <br><br><i>
  <b> “You think of everything.”<br>“I simply think of you. You are everything.”</b>
</i> <br><br>The only thing that bothered me was the one error I spotted. This book is written so perfectly with so many details that require hours upon hours of research that this one tiny thing kept gnawing at me. It was the mistaken use of the word nephew when the relationship would have been that of a brother. Not a major deal considering that the age gap sometimes makes that correlation feel a bit odd, but since this book required such an eye for detail the fact that this was not caught just bothered me.<br><br>Gabriel’s journey was beautifully told and being able to see the transformation of what we saw at the start of this series to what we saw at the end was simply beautiful. The last moments of this book had my heart breaking. The amount of love that he carried within his heart for Julia is something that just takes your breath away.<br><br><i>
  <b> “I love this man with all my heart. I’d give my life for him. Id’ give anything for him.”</b>
</i> <br><br><br><br><br><br>========================================<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380408686ra/799700.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="927517504016758848" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

    <a title="Jo" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/8278010-jo"><img alt="Jo" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1352109855p2/8278010.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/567863773?book_show_action=true">Mar 22, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jo" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jo" href="/user/show/8278010-jo">Jo</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/18368537-gabriel-s-redemption">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer567863773" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10562651378362697920"><br/><b>**5 " I can't believe it's over" kind of stars **</b><br/><br/><br/><b>
  <i>"For you, my love, I would endeavor to pluck the stars from the sky, only to shower them at your feet."</i>
</b><br/><br/>By far, this book was one of the most anticipated books of this year I was eagerly expecting it's release.<br/>The conclusion of the series that introduces us to the beautiful and mesmerizing love story of...<br/><br/><b>Julianne</b><br/><a href='http://imageshack.us/photo/my-images/713/kwo.gif/' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1386379355ra/7351129.gif' alt='Image Hosted by ImageShack.us' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/>and<br/><br/><b>Gabriel</b><br/><a href='http://imageshack.us/photo/my-images/593/q4c.gif/' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1386379355ra/7351130.gif' alt='Image Hosted by ImageShack.us' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Our passionate couple is over the moon. They just married and they never been happier.<br/>Still, they're are shadows tr</span>
  <span id="freeText10562651378362697920" style="display:none"><br><b>**5 " I can't believe it's over" kind of stars **</b><br><br><br><b>
  <i>"For you, my love, I would endeavor to pluck the stars from the sky, only to shower them at your feet."</i>
</b><br><br>By far, this book was one of the most anticipated books of this year I was eagerly expecting it's release.<br>The conclusion of the series that introduces us to the beautiful and mesmerizing love story of...<br><br><b>Julianne</b><br><a href="http://imageshack.us/photo/my-images/713/kwo.gif/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1386379355ra/7351129.gif" alt="Image Hosted by ImageShack.us" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>and<br><br><b>Gabriel</b><br><a href="http://imageshack.us/photo/my-images/593/q4c.gif/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1386379355ra/7351130.gif" alt="Image Hosted by ImageShack.us" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Our passionate couple is over the moon. They just married and they never been happier.<br>Still, they're are shadows trying to lurk their happiness. <br>Christa is set on spreading rumors about them. In her mind she always gets what she wants, and she set her price on him. <br>Also his past it's still haunting him and he must seek answers to gain some peace with his Beatrice.<br>Obstacles keeps appearing and they're more united than ever to overcome them all.<br><br>The evolution of both characters is just amazing!! Julia is more mature and gradually becoming more sure of herself. And Gabriel, that could be so selfish, now is completely selfless regarding Julia. It shows even in his relationship with his family and friends.<br><br>I just love this couple so much. Their love is just a beauty to behold! Their devotion to each other, passion and fated to be together.<br><br><a href="http://imageshack.us/photo/my-images/822/orwg.jpg/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1386379355i/7351131.jpg" alt="Image Hosted by ImageShack.us" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>The way they see each other and connect at such a higher level, is just B-E-A-U-T-I-F-U-L. Seriously is the word that keeps popping in my mind in each of the 3 books of the series.<br>It's one of the few romances, that their work is pivotal to the story. They're Dante specialist and we see how much they love it and how it brought them together. And the parallels between their story and their studies is just amazing.The details of the paintings, history and music, elevates even more this already unique story.<br><br>Now all adding the exquisite writing of Reynard, it just makes reading this trilogy an unforgettable and one of a kind reading experience. <br><br>And that ending? PERFECTION!<br><br><br>I can't recommend this series enough :)<br><br><br>*egalley kindly given via Netgalley in exchange of an honest review! THANK YOU!*<br></span>

And because of that I'm going to give this book 5 stars for the whole overall experience of this series.<br><br><b>SERIES:</b><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/10140661.Gabriel_s_Inferno__Gabriel_s_Inferno___1_" title="Gabriel's Inferno (Gabriel's Inferno, #1) by Sylvain Reynard" rel="nofollow noopener">

I set the bar higher for an author who is continuing a series, and to WoW! me isn’t an automatic, or an easy gimme.<br/>You c</span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/665775075?book_show_action=true">Jul 12, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Shurrn" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Shurrn" href="/user/show/22115857-shurrn">Shurrn</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22115857-shurrn?shelf=i-lol-moments">i-lol-moments</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22115857-shurrn?shelf=z-own-for-ipad">z-own-for-ipad</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22115857-shurrn?shelf=z-own-for-kindle">z-own-for-kindle</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22115857-shurrn?shelf=c-billionaires-and-executives">c-billionaires-and-executives</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22115857-shurrn?shelf=romance-modern">romance-modern</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22115857-shurrn?shelf=series-completed">series-completed</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer665775075" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18033204681186614804"><b>The Gabriel's Inferno series is my unicorn - I LOVED the first book, then I endured a seemingly endless spiral of mediocrity, religious allegory, & angst as I saw it through to the conclusion...</b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380429778ra/861201.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>Julia’s heart nearly cracked under the weight of her realization that her love had not healed him.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote> <b>
  <u>Really quickly:</u>
</b> <br/>If you liked the second book in this series, I think you'll really enjoy this book...<br/>But, if you're like me & the second book left a bad taste in your mouth... Stay away from</span>
  <span id="freeText18033204681186614804" style="display:none"><b>The Gabriel's Inferno series is my unicorn - I LOVED the first book, then I endured a seemingly endless spiral of mediocrity, religious allegory, &amp; angst as I saw it through to the conclusion...</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380429778ra/861201.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>Julia’s heart nearly cracked under the weight of her realization that her love had not healed him.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote> <b>
  <u>Really quickly:</u>
</b> <br>If you liked the second book in this series, I think you'll really enjoy this book...<br>But, if you're like me &amp; the second book left a bad taste in your mouth... Stay away from this.<br><br>I feel like this book took so long to come out, and had so much lead up to it's publication, that there was no way it could possibly live up to reader's expectations... There was so much information which needed to be cleared up...<br><br>So many characters needed conclusions,<br>So much angst had to be resolved,<br>The mysterious past of Gabriel had to be revealed,<br>...and once all of that was done, the author had to convince us that Julia and Gabriel could have a happily ever after.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380410232ra/804048.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Don’t cry, my sweet girl. You’re my Beatrice and my sticky little leaf and my beautiful wife. I’m sorry I’ve been such a bastard. I wanted to show you how important you are to me. You are my most precious masterpiece.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote> That's a tall order.<br><br>I'm pleased to say that everything was resolved in the final installment of the Gabriel's Inferno Series...<br><br>But was it satisfactory?<br>Not for me, personally...<br>I don't need everything neat and tidy to the point of sterility, but that is the ending provided to us.<br><br>If I could go back and do it all over again, I would have been perfectly happy to read the first book and be done with the series.<br><br>That being said, the writing is still spectacular and Gabriel Emerson is still a swoony sonofabitch... So it wasn't all bad.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1386980515i/7499020._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>

          </span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/507032804?book_show_action=true">Jan 15, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" href="/user/show/4197769-jacqueline-s-reads">Jacqueline&#39;s Reads</a>
      </span>

          marked it as did-not-finish




        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer507032804" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13521440420831593644"><b>DNF… MAY RETURN AT A FUTURE DATE</b><br/><br/>Oh god it’s killing me. Have you ever waited so long to get your hands on a book? I did! For this one and when the GOD’s opened up and yes, I got a PAPERBACK ARC, I think I had a heart attack. I loved book 1, Gabriel’s Inferno and yes book 2 was a bit disappointing, but I figure that was just the filler book.<br/><br/><b>SAD TO SAY… I HAD HUGE expectations for Gabriel’s Redemption</b><br/><br/>SIGH SIGH SIGH SIGH… WAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAA<br/><br/>I am going to describe this book in two words. READY?!<br/><br/><b>BOR</b></span>
  <span id="freeText13521440420831593644" style="display:none"><b>DNF… MAY RETURN AT A FUTURE DATE</b><br /><br />Oh god it’s killing me. Have you ever waited so long to get your hands on a book? I did! For this one and when the GOD’s opened up and yes, I got a PAPERBACK ARC, I think I had a heart attack. I loved book 1, Gabriel’s Inferno and yes book 2 was a bit disappointing, but I figure that was just the filler book.<br /><br /><b>SAD TO SAY… I HAD HUGE expectations for Gabriel’s Redemption</b><br /><br />SIGH SIGH SIGH SIGH… WAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAA<br /><br />I am going to describe this book in two words. READY?!<br /><br /><b>BORING &amp; LONG</b><br /><br />Usually I crave long books and I can’t get enough it, but there was no story line. I felt like I was this patient in the waiting room just waiting for my turn, you know something to happen. Come on Gabriel, go crazy, do something that makes me want to hate you and love you at the same time.<br /><br />I figure the beginning was just a lot of intro stuff. So I bore through it, but the thing is, the book is so long that 10% is like 30% of a normal book I read. UGGGGGGGGGGGGG<br /><br />I got through to the 50% mark. There was hardly any steam, I mean, there’s plenty of sex, but not really. I don’t need a detailed description, but what’s the point in having all that sex if there isn’t going to be any explanation? I dunno, hard to explain.<br /><br />As to all the high reviews… this is all I can say <br /><br /><b>I just don’t get it</b><br /><br />So, it’s going back on my shelf and who knows I may pick it up on a rainy day.<br /><br /><i>An ARC was provided in exchange for an honest review</i><br /></span>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('UdEzDKL6Vfgy1Xc4xT9a5eDn/UreFK39WOeqQTV7kihRb5ITLUB8UZgdRyuFMmF1eFtO/Pvp0asDG6fmWaUssw==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('Uv+4yPKWbprz7ZtL6QynLms62EY/6BQ5gZK/NEMsNcxSQRnXfSxHM1klq1ipAZy+84Zr8BoVaG/abrKTL/KLVw==')})
  }
//]]>

<span id="freeTextContainer16254233397349063642">"Gabriel's Promise" has been released and is now available across platforms: <a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='https://amzn.to/2Y6ah10'>https://amzn.to/2Y6ah10</a><br/><br/>My New York Times Best Selling Gabriel Series has been acquired by Passionflix. You can meet the cast, read the most recent update, and learn how to sign up for Passionflix here: <a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='http://sylvainreynard.com/film-series-news/'>http://sylvainr</a></span>
  <span id="freeText16254233397349063642" style="display:none">"Gabriel's Promise" has been released and is now available across platforms: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://amzn.to/2Y6ah10">https://amzn.to/2Y6ah10</a><br /><br />My New York Times Best Selling Gabriel Series has been acquired by Passionflix. "Gabriel's Inferno" is available now on Passionflix.com. "Gabriel's Rapture" will resume filming in 2021. You can meet the cast, read the most recent update, and learn how to sign up for Passionflix here: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://sylvainreynard.com/film-series-news/">http://sylvainreynard.com/film-series...</a><br /><br />You can view the trailer to the third and final part here: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=mjPUGem9SaY">https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=mjPUG...</a><br /><br />Huffington Post Books ranked "Gabriel's Inferno" as the best teacher/student romance novel. <br /><br />My latest book, "The Man in the Black Suit, (#TMitBS), is a contemporary romance/suspense standalone novel, set in Paris: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://t.co/pdpHlvVtjO">https://t.co/pdpHlvVtjO</a><br /><br />The Florentine Series is now complete. Each paperback edition has additional content. Audio and ebooks are also available.<br /><br />The second book in that series, "The Raven," was nominated by RT Magazine as Best Paranormal Romance Suspense novel of 2015.<br /><br />I am honoured to have had my novels appear on the New York Times and USAToday Bestseller lists. <br /><br />I was a Semifinalist for Best Author in the 2011 and 2012 Goodreads Choice Awards. "Gabriel's Inferno" was a Semifinalist for Best Romance in 2011 and "Gabriel's Rapture" was a Finalist for Best Romance in 2012, in the Goodreads Choice Awards, as well. The final novel in The Gabriel Series, "Gabriel's Redemption," debuted at #6 on the New York Times Bestseller list. It was a Finalist for a 2014 Goodreads Choice Award as Best Romance.<br /><br />I'm interested in the way literature can help us explore aspects of the human condition - particularly suffering, sex, love, faith, and redemption. My favourite stories are those in which a character takes a journey, either a physical journey to a new and exciting place, or a personal journey in which he or she learns something about himself/herself. <br /><br />I'm also interested in how aesthetic elements such as art, architecture, food, drink, and music can be used to tell a story or to illuminate the traits of a particular character. In my writing, I combine all of these elements with the themes of redemption, forgiveness, and the transformative power of goodness.<br /><br />I try to use my platform as an author to raise awareness about the following charities: Now I Lay Me Down to Sleep Foundation, WorldVision, Alex's Lemonade Stand, and Covenant House. <br /><br />For more information, see my Twitter account or my website.<br /><br />I also do not check my Goodreads email.<br /><br />To email me, please use the below addy. <br />info@sylvainreynard.com</span>
